# Translation file for QueueMetrics - en_US

- The name WombatDialer is a product and should be left unaltered. 
- The acronym "CSV" should be unaltered.
- The acronym "AMO" stands for Assisted Manual Outbound


## Language pack

General information about this language pack. The language name should be written in the
language itself, and will appear in the drop-down language selector.

    00-LanguageName=Romanian
    
Do not change the items below:

    dateformat_complete=MMMM dd yyyy, HH:mm
    dateformat_completeshort=MM/dd - HH:mm:ss
    dateformat_date=MMMM dd yyyy
    dateformat_flow=1
    dateformat_time=HH:mm:ss
    dateformat_timeshort=HH:mm

## Editor of security keys

Description of security keys:

    # 游놓 keydesc_agaw -> User can access AGAW facades (for agents).
    keydesc_agaw=?Utilizatorul poate accesa fa탵adele AGAW (pentru agen탵i).

    # 游놓 keydesc_agent -> User is an agent and sees agent page
    keydesc_agent=?Utilizatorul este un agent 탳i vede pagina agentului
    # 游놓 keydesc_agrep -> User can filter reports by agent
    keydesc_agrep=?Utilizatorul poate filtra rapoartele dup캒 agent
    # 游놓 keydesc_autoanswer_phone -> User can toggle Auto Answer on the softphone
    keydesc_autoanswer_phone=?Utilizatorul poate activa/dezactiva r캒spunsul automat pe softphone
    # 游놓 keydesc_batch_add -> Can add calls to an open batch
    keydesc_batch_add=?Poate ad캒uga apeluri la un batch deschis
    # 游놓 keydesc_batch_adm -> Creates and closes batches for exporting audio
    keydesc_batch_adm=?Creeaz캒 탳i 칥nchide batch-uri pentru exportul audio
